### PRO TOUR KHANS OF TARKIR


TOP STANDARD DECKS A-N
======================



![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)

Wizards of the Coast




October 12, 2014
 











 Listed below are all the Standard decks that earned 21 points or more in the Constructed rounds of Pro Tour *Khans of Tarkir*. Each deck is preceded by a short explanation of how the deck works.




**Jeskai Wins**



Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.






#### Marco Cammilluzzi


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-0b5ff30edf02cb5c49740bab1e9b6050.txt?n=Marco%20Cammilluzzi)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Flooded+Strand)


















**Temur Monsters**



The deck uses mana acceleration to quickly pump out some of the biggest, scariest creatures in the format.






#### Pedro Carvalho


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-389494fa186b7588ae4562d455159cd3.txt?n=Pedro%20Carvalho)

**Jeskai Wins**



Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.






#### Justin Cheung


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-21cfcd6d53e8ea3eb8269a4220736950.txt?n=Justin%20Cheung)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Temple+of+Triumph)


















**Blue-Black Control**




 A pure control strategy, this two-color deck wants to remove all of the opponent's threats one-by-one, pulling ahead on cards with [Dig Through Time](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Dig+Through+Time) and [Jace's Ingenuity](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Jace%27s+Ingenuity). [Perilous Vault](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Perilous+Vault) is the sweeper of choice, and can reset virtually any board to the control player's favor.







#### Andrew Cuneo


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-b4ec18980b908dd8b1281800b84f5ecc.txt?n=Andrew%20Cuneo)

**Mardu Planeswalkers**



This midrange deck generates most of its value from its Planeswalkers, then uses a suite of removal and disruption to keep the opponent off-balance while the Planeswalkers do their work.






#### Pierre Dagen


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-a081ab3a11dc960832b4a0d2b9c03be7.txt?n=Pierre%20Dagen)

**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Leonardo De Castro

**Blue-Black Control**




 A pure control strategy, this two-color deck wants to remove all of the opponent's threats one-by-one, pulling ahead on cards with [Dig Through Time](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Dig+Through+Time) and [Jace's Ingenuity](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Jace%27s+Ingenuity).







#### Ivan Floch


#####

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Prognostic+Sphinx)


















**Jeskai Ascendancy Combo**




 The format's only true combo deck, [Jeskai Ascendancy](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Jeskai+Ascendancy) uses its namesake card along with creatures that make mana to churn through its deck, casting spell after spell before ultimately killing with a large attacking creature, decking from [Altar of the Brood](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Altar+of+the+Brood), or any number of ways. [Retraction Helix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Retraction+Helix) and a zero-cost spell make the combo repeatable as many times as necessary.







#### Eric Froehlich


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-a415b8bfa769bebcfe4952c2611711fe.txt?n=Eric%20Froehlich)

**Jeskai Wins**



Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.






#### Francesco Giorgio


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-49d301ae6f3f937a0c655fda7cfbe221.txt?n=Francesco%20Giorgio)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Temple+of+Triumph)


















**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Danny Goldstein


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-b95236275c900b743f95468d1b8d5371.txt?n=Danny%20Goldstein)

**Mardu Midrange**



This midrange deck generates most of its value from its Planeswalkers, then uses a suite of removal and disruption to keep the opponent off-balance while the Planeswalkers and efficient, frightening creatures do their work.






#### Nathan Herkimer


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-d5a1c934e4ec7573979d2041bd92cec1.txt?n=Nathan%20Herkimer)

**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Jonathan Hickerson


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-a5ba818a78c10c13c156c457d6c13f5d.txt?n=Jonathan%20Hickerson)

**Red-White Heroic**



Brutally fast and efficient, this deck utilizes the heroic mechanic to turn small, fast red and white creatures into large, fast red and white creatures.






#### Yoshihiko Ikawa


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-de859d76a6ed837832fd2f11f322105e.txt?n=Yoshihiko%20Ikawa)

**Jeskai Wins**



Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.






#### Maciej Janik


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-89dfab408f632ad2d416bc74be46bd8c.txt?n=Maciej%20Janik)

**Naya Midrange**




 This midrange deck generates most of its value from its Planeswalkers, accelerating them out with green mana creatures like [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid). Some of the format's strongest creatures let the deck also go big.







#### Adam Jansen


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-9ae40630f4aa4fbfcb3b9023f824bf6d.txt?n=Adam%20Jansen)

**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Alexander John


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-4ca2c253de3bbfb26bbd51625f05136b.txt?n=Alexander%20John)

**Jeskai Wins**



Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.






#### Jadine Klomparens


#####

**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Elvish+Mystic)


















**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Ari Lax


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-b2893ee1908c28edc6b9fd864aa6d4ed.txt?n=Ari%20Lax)

**Abzan Midrange**




 This [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid)/[Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) deck is packed full of value and individually powerful spells, trying to jam many of the format's best cards into the same 75-card decklist.







#### Aaron Lewis


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-2e5d9809ad1fad2b5ccddcfceadabe59.txt?n=Aaron%20Lewis)

![](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?type=card&name=Thoughtseize)


















**Abzan Aggro**




 This more aggressive take on Abzan often forgoes [Sylvan Caryatid](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Sylvan+Caryatid) and [Courser of Kruphix](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Courser+of+Kruphix) for more aggressively-minded creatures, such as [Rakshasa Deathdealer](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Rakshasa+Deathdealer) and [Herald of Torment](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Herald+of+Torment), trying to put opponents off balance with some of the strongest creatures at every point in the curve.







#### Josh McClain


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-7f3d5b3627d11eac29d93fd8c961b56f.txt?n=Josh%20McClain)

**Jeskai Wins**



Using a significant compliment of burn spells and hard-hitting creatures, Jeskai Wins often ends the game in a flurry of damage. It's also capable of adapting a controlling role on occasion if the situation calls for it.






#### Andrea Mengucci


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-650a79f68cadae1482edbff6355d3066.txt?n=Andrea%20Mengucci)

**Unwritten Devotion**




 This green and black devotion deck utilizes [Nykthos, Shrine to Nyx](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Nykthos%2C+Shrine+to+Nyx) to make a ton of mana, supports a constellation sub-theme, AND goes for the big score with [See the Unwritten](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=See+the+Unwritten).







#### Makahito Mihara


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-a01440f4d19519b67f609b4a69197f49.txt?n=Makahito%20Mihara)

**Red-White Tokens**




[Hordeling Outburst](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Hordeling+Outburst) and [Goblin Rabblemaster](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Goblin+Rabblemaster) team up with [Monastery Swiftspear](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Pages/Card/Details.aspx?name=Monastery+Swiftspear) and a large helping of burn to quickly drop the opponent to zero.
